  868|    210|fn emit_addr(ctx: &mut CodegenContext, out: &mut String, expr: &syn::Expr, local_vars: &mut HashMap<String, (Type, LocalKind)>) -> Result<(String, Type), String> {

  874|    139|                 if let LocalKind::Ptr(ptr_name) = kind {

  880|     12|                      out.push_str(&format!("    llvm.store {}, {} : {}, !llvm.ptr\n", ssa_name, tmp_alloca, mlir_ty));
  881|     12|                      Ok((tmp_alloca, ty))
  882|       |                  } else {
  883|      0|                       Err(format!("Cannot take address of variable {}", name))

   17|    276|fn process_block(block: &mut SaltBlock, evaluator: &mut Evaluator) -> Result<(), EvalError> {
   18|  1.75k|    for stmt in &mut block.stmts {

   35|  1.24k|fn process_syn_stmt(stmt: &mut syn::Stmt, evaluator: &mut Evaluator) -> Result<(), EvalError> {
   36|  1.24k|        match stmt {
   37|    866|            syn::Stmt::Local(local) => {
   38|       |                // Heuristic: If it's a `let` binding, we try to optimize it (Case B).
   39|       |                // If we had `const` or `salt.constant` we would treat it as Case A (Mandatory).
   40|       |                
   41|       |                // For now, scan assignment: let x = <expr>;
   42|       |                // If <expr> evaluates to a constant, register x in the table and replace <expr>.
   43|       |                
   44|    866|                if let Some(init) = &mut local.init {
   45|       |                    // Opportunity: Try to eval
   46|    866|                    match evaluator.eval_expr(&init.expr) {
   47|    202|                        Ok(val) => {
   48|       |                            // It evaluated!
   49|       |                            // 1. Register so future uses can see it (within this scope/flow - simplifying to global for MVP)
   50|    202|                            if let syn::Pat::Ident(pat_ident) = &local.pat {
                                                                 ^42
   51|     42|                                evaluator.constant_table.insert(pat_ident.ident.to_string(), val.clone());
   52|    160|                            }
   53|       |                            
   54|       |                            // 2. Optimization: Replace the expression with the literal
   55|    202|                            *init.expr = value_to_expr(val);
   56|       |                        },
   57|    664|                        Err(_) => {
   58|    664|                            // Fallback: It's runtime code. Do nothing.
   59|    664|                        }
   60|       |                    }
   61|      0|                }
   62|       |            }
   63|    383|            syn::Stmt::Expr(expr, _) => {
   64|       |                 // Try to fold expressions too
   65|    383|                 if let Ok(val) = evaluator.eval_expr(expr) {
                                         ^2
   66|      2|                     *expr = value_to_expr(val);
   67|    381|                 }
   68|       |            }

   74|    204|fn value_to_expr(val: ConstValue) -> Expr {
   75|    204|    match val {
   76|    174|        ConstValue::Integer(i) => Expr::Lit(syn::ExprLit {
   77|    174|            attrs: vec![],
   78|    174|            lit: Lit::Int(LitInt::new(&i.to_string(), proc_macro2::Span::call_site())),
   79|    174|        }),
